***торопить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:торопить.html>торопи́ть</a> (8323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Vasmer adduces <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τρέπω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trépō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*terkʷ-</i>), and possibly <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τέρπω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">térpō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*terp-</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торопить.html>торопи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">toropítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поторопить.html>поторопи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hurry, to hasten, to precipitate, to rush
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:торопить.html>торопи́ть</a></b> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>toropítʹ</b> kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hurry someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:торопить.html>торо́пит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>torópit</b> menjá s okončánijem rabóty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is hurrying me to finish my work</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:торопить.html>торо́пит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответ.html>отве́том</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>torópit</b> menjá s otvétom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is hurrying/pressing me for an answer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:торопить.html>торопи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:событие.html>собы́тия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>toropítʹ</b> sobýtija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rush things</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">hurry, hasten</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подгонять.html>подгоня́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podgonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">bring nearer?</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приближать.html>приближа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">približátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***торопиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:торопиться.html>торопи́ться</a> (1508)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торопить.html>торопи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">toropítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торопиться.html>торопи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">toropítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поторопиться.html>поторопи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hurry, to be in a hurry, to hasten
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:торопиться.html>торопи́тесь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:некогда.html>не́когда</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туда.html>туда́</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Toropítesʹ</b>, rebjáta! Nam nékogda idtí tudá!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Hurry</b>, guys! We don't have any time to go there!</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***торпеда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:торпеда.html>торпе́да</a> (22157)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торпеда.html>торпе́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">torpéda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торпеда.html>торпе́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торпеда.html>торпе́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торпеда.html>торпе́д</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торпедный.html>торпе́дный</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:торфяной.html>торфяно́й</a> (29284)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торф.html>торф</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">torf</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-яно́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-janój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торфяной.html>торфяно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">torfjanój</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> peat

***торчать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:торчать.html>торча́ть</a> (1360)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:торчать.html>торча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">torčátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to stick out, to protrude, to jut out</li>
<li>to stand on end, to bristle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of hair</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to loiter, to stick around, to hang around</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel a euphoria, to get a kick, to get high</li></ol>

***тоска.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоска́</a> (1849)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tъska</i>, which is perhaps related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тощий.html>то́щий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тискать.html>ти́скать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tískatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоска́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">toská</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоски́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>melancholy, depression</li>
<li>boredom, ennui, weariness</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уныние.html>уны́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">unýnije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:депрессия.html>депре́ссия</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">deprɛ́ssija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меланхолия.html>меланхо́лия</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">melanxólija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хандра.html>хандра́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xandrá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоскливо.html>тоскливо</a> (6409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тоскливый.html>тоскли́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tosklívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тоскливо.html>тоскли́во</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tosklívo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>drearily</li>
<li>sadly, in a sad voice
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляде́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тоскливо.html>тоскли́во</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gljadétʹ <b>tosklívo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to look wistfully</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>dully</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тоскливо.html>тоскли́во</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tosklívo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>one feels miserable/depressed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тоскливо.html>тоскли́во</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>tosklívo</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he feels miserable/depressed</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тоскливо.html>тоскли́во</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляде́ть</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>tosklívo</b> na éto gljadétʹ!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">it makes one so miserable to see this!; the sight of this is so depressing!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>one is bored
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тоскливо.html>тоскли́во</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú zdesʹ <b>tosklívo</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">this place is boring for him</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ol><li><i>нареч.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоскливый.html>тоскли́вый</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:скучно.html>ску́чно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:безрадостный.html>безра́достно</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

***тосковать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тосковать.html>тоскова́ть</a> (7017)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тосковать.html>тоскова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">toskovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be sad/melancholic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тосковать.html>тоску́ет</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On tam <b>toskújet</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>is/feels miserable</b> there.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be bored</li>
<li>to long, to pine, to miss, to have a nostalgia, to grieve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тосковать.html>тоску́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́гу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná óčenʹ <b>toskújet</b> po drúgu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She <b>misses</b> her friend very much.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тосковать.html>тоскова́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:родина.html>ро́дине</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>toskovátʹ</b> po ródine</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be homesick</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затосковать.html>затоскова́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zatoskovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***тоскующий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тосковать.html>тоску́ющий</a> (7017)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тосковать.html>тоску́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">toskújuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тосковать.html>тоскова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">toskovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тосковать.html>тоску́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">toskújuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>yearning, wistful</li>
<li>grieving</li></ol>

***тот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> (8)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*tas</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*só</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*séh₂</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*tód</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">this, that</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">tas</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">tas</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">ta</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">स</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">se</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">the</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tot</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>demonstrative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>that, those</li>
<li>the one</li>
<li>the other</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóčka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точечный.html>то́чечный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóčečnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> point
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:точечный.html>то́чечный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бомбовый.html>бо́мбовый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tóčečnyj</b> bómbovyj udár</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pointed bombing/strike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:точечный.html>то́чечный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заряд.html>заря́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tóčečnyj</b> zarjád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">point charge</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:точечный.html>то́чечный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:источник.html>исто́чник</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tóčečnyj</b> istóčnik svéta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">spotlight source; pinpoint light source</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:точечный.html>то́чечный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:массаж.html>масса́ж</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tóčečnyj</b> massáž</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pressure point massage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:точечный.html>то́чечная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>цель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tóčečnaja</b> celʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">point target</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:точечный.html>то́чечное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>отве́рстие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tóčečnoje</b> otvérstije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pinhole</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:точечный.html>то́чечный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прогноз.html>прогно́з</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tóčečnyj</b> prognóz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">single-value prediction</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dot, dotty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:точечный.html>то́чечная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:диаграмма.html>диагра́мма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tóčečnaja</b> diagrámma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dot chart</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́ло</a> (19671)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">točítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">točílo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́ла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́л</a></b>)

<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

***точить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́ть</a> (11052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Follows from the diachronic convergence of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tъčiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to point, to sharpen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which ultimately continues PIE <span class="Latinx" lang="ine-pro">*tewk-</span> (“to hew” gt; “to shove, to weave, to seed”), with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tоčiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drain, to protract</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from PIE <span class="Latinx" lang="ine-pro">*tekʷ-</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flow, to run</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The first form is an iterative derivative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ткнуть.html>ткнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tknutʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to poke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> while the second is a causative derivative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:течь.html>течь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tečʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">točítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to sharpen, to hone, to whet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зу́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>točítʹ</b> zúby na</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bear a grudge against</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наточить.html>наточи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">natočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заточить.html>заточи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zatočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поточи́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to produce, to make <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">using a lathe</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выточить.html>вы́точить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výtočitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wear away, to wear down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to nag</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">točítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:источить.html>источи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to emit, to exude (smell, light, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shed (tears)</li></ol>

***точка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чка</a> (702)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">taškas</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>period, dot, full stop</li>
<li>point
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прикосновение.html>прикоснове́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tóčka</b> prikosnovénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>point</b> of contact</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>dot, <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for Morse code; colloquially dit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>  “Мой <a href = vnd.unilang:адрес.html>а́дрес</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:советский.html>Советский</a> Союз”:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вы</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чки</a></b>-тире́ <a href = vnd.unilang:телеграфный.html>телегра́фные</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:искать.html>ищи́те</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стройка.html>стро́йках</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vy, <b>tóčki</b>-tirɛ́ telegráfnyje, iščíte na strójkax menjá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">(You) telegraphic <b>dots</b> and dashes, search me on building sites.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чка</a>!</strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóčka!</span>)

***точно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:точно.html>то́чно</a> (312)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точный.html>то́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">тъчьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tŭčĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:точно.html>то́чно</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóčno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">točno</i>/<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh"><a href = vnd.unilang:точно.html>то́чно</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:точно.html>то́чно</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóčno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точно.html>то́чно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóčno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-то́чно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)точне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-то́чно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)точне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>exactly, precisely, accurately</li>
<li>definitely</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точно.html>то́чно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóčno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>exactly!, yes!, bingo!</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точно.html>то́чно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóčno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>as though, as if</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точно.html>то́чно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóčno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точный.html>то́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точный.html>то́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точность.html>то́чность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóčnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точность.html>то́чности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точность.html>то́чности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точность.html>то́чностей</a></b>)

<ol><li>exactness, precision, accuracy, punctuality (the state of being exact)</li></ol>

***точный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:точный.html>то́чный</a> (1098)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">točítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sharpen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; original meaning "sharpened".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точный.html>то́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóčnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)точне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)точне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>exact, precise, accurate

<li>correct</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тошнить.html>тошни́ть</a> (9587)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошный.html>то́шный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóšnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошнить.html>тошни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tošnítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause nausea
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лекарство.html>лека́рства</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́льно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тошнить.html>тошни́ло</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pósle nóvovo lekárstva menjá sílʹno <b>tošnílo</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">After taking my new medication, I <b>felt</b> very <b>nauseous</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тошно.html>то́шно</a> (10115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошный.html>то́шный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóšnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошно.html>то́шно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóšno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> disgustingly, sickeningly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> miserably</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошно.html>то́шно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóšno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> it is nauseating, it is sickening</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> it is miserable, it is wretched</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> it is anguishing</li></ol>

***тошнота.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тошнота.html>тошнота́</a> (6555)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошный.html>то́шный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóšnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ота́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-otá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошнота.html>тошнота́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tošnotá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошнота.html>тошноты́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошнота.html>тошно́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошнота.html>тошно́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sickness, nausea (qualmishness; as, sickness of stomach)</li>
<li>loathing</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошный.html>то́шный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóšnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nauseating</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:творить.html>твори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tvorítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to create</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошнотворный.html>тошнотво́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tošnotvórnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тошнотво́рнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тошнотво́рней</b>)
